+ Professional Services</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV at any given point in time represents the forward-looking revenues for the next 12 months from all subscription services currently supplied to clients. Professional services are revenues derived from project-based consulting and implementation services.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV plus professional services was $2,219.2 million at May&#160;31, 2024, compared with $2,120.1 million at May&#160;31, 2023. Organic ASV plus professional services was $2,220.4 million at May&#160;31, 2024, up $105.6 million from the prior year, for a growth rate </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">of 5.0%. Organic ASV plus professional services increased </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">$11.7 m</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">illion over the last three months. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%">Buy-side and sell-side organic ASV growth rates for the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%">third</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%"> quarter of fiscal </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%">2024</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%"> were 5.3% and 3.7%, respectively. Buy-side clients, including institutional asset managers, wealth managers, asset owners, hedge funds, partners, and corporate clients, accounted for 82% of organic ASV. The remaining organic ASV came from sell-side firms, including broker-dealers, banking and advisory, and private equity and venture capital firms. Supplementary tables covering organic buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates may be found on the last page of this press release. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Segment</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> Revenues and ASV</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Americas region was $1,417.1 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of $1,344.7 million. Americas revenues for the quarter increased to $356.5 million compared with $337.7 million in the third quarter of last year. The Americas region's organic revenues growth rate was 5.5%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the EMEA region was $565.7 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of $541.3 million. Third Quarter Fiscal 2024</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Client count as of May&#160;31, 2024 was 8,029, a net increase of 9 clients in the past three months, with increases driven by wealth, corporates, and partners. Quarterly free cash flow increased to $216.9 million compared with $192.6 million a year ago, an increase of 12.6%, primarily driven by an increase in net cash provided by operating activities.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">A quarterly dividend of $39.6 million, or $1.04 per share, was paid on June&#160;20, 2024, to holders of record of FactSet&#8217;s common stock at the close of business on May&#160;31, 2024. This represented a 6% increase in the regular quarterly dividend from the $0.98 per share paid in the previous quarter and marks the 25th consecutive year the Company has increased dividends on a stock split-adjusted basis.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet announced the release of its Transcript Assistant, a GenAI-powered, conversational chatbot that accelerates in-depth research and analysis of earnings call transcripts.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet announced the release of its Portfolio Commentary solution. Powered by large language models (LLMs), Portfolio Commentary significantly reduces the challenging, time-consuming, and nuanced process of writing attribution summaries manually. Instead, with the click of a button, users can generate baseline and source-linked portfolio commentary for any attribution report in approximately 30-60 seconds.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">In addition, in June 2024, FactSet made a $12.5 million investment in Aidentified, Inc., a leading AI-powered prospecting and relationship intelligence platform for financial services professionals. Aidentified provides financial advisors, marketing teams, and other sales professionals with tools to identify, qualify, and convert new client relationships. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Share Repurchase Program</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">FactSet repurchased 135,150 shares of its common stock for $59.8 million at an average price of $442.12 during the third quarter of fiscal 2024 under the Company&#8217;s share repurchase program.
